  export class $wnet_app_object extends $mol_store< Object > {
    
    repo(): $wnet_app_object_repo {
      throw new Error('Not implemented')
    }

    id() {
      return this.value( '_id' )
    }

    deleted( next?: boolean ) {
      return this.value( 'deleted' , next ) ?? false
    }
    
    createdAt() { return this.value( 'createdAt' ) }

    updatedAt() { return this.value( 'updatedAt' ) }
    
    title_raw( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'title_raw' , next ) ?? '' 
    }
    
    street( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'street' , next ) ?? '' 
    }
    
    house( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'house' , next ) ?? '' 
    }
    
    @ $mol_mem
    title() {
      if ( this.street() || this.house() ) return `${ this.street() } ${ this.house() }`.trim()
      if ( !this.title_raw() ) return `${ this.createdAt() }`
      
      const parsed_object = $wnet_app_measure_parse.object( this.title_raw() )
      return `${ parsed_object.street } ${ parsed_object.house }`
    }

    type( next?: Object['type'] ) {
      return this.value( 'type' , next ) ?? 'apartment' 
    }
    
    ftp_host( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_host' , next ) ?? '' 
    }
    
    ftp_user( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_user' , next ) ?? '' 
    }
    
    ftp_pass( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_pass' , next ) ?? ''
    }
    
    ftp_port( next?: number ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_port' , next ) ?? 21
    }
    
    ftp_sync_enabled( next?: boolean ) {
      if ( next ) {
        this.ftp_sync_time( new $mol_time_moment( new Date(0) ) )
      }
      return this.value( 'ftp_sync_enabled' , next ) ?? false
    }
    
    ftp_sync_time( next?: $mol_time_moment ) {
      const str = this.value( 'ftp_sync_time' , next && next.toString() )
      return str ? new $mol_time_moment( new Date(str) ) : null
    }
    
    ftp_sync_files( next?: string[] ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_sync_files' , next ) ?? []
    }
    
    ftp_sync_progress(next?: number) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_sync_progress' , next ) ?? 1
    }
    
    ftp_sync_error( next?: string ) {
      return this.value( 'ftp_sync_error' , next ) ?? ''
    }
    
    ftp_sync_updating() {
      return this.value( 'ftp_sync_updating' ) ?? false
    }
    
    places() {
      console.log(222)
      return this.repo().domain().place().list().filter( place => place.object().id() === this.id()  )
    }
    
    @ $mol_fiber.method
    refresh() {
      const object = this.$.$wnet_app_transport.load( `object/${ this.id() }` ) as Object
      const dict = this.repo().data()
      this.repo().data({
        ... dict,
        [object._id!]: {
          ... this.data(),
          ftp_sync_enabled: object.ftp_sync_enabled,
          ftp_sync_error: object.ftp_sync_error,
          ftp_sync_progress: object.ftp_sync_progress,
          ftp_sync_time: object.ftp_sync_time,
          ftp_sync_updating: object.ftp_sync_updating,
          title_raw: object.title_raw,
        }
      })
    }

    @ $mol_fiber.method
    reload() {
      this.$.$wnet_app_transport.save(`object/reload/${ this.id() }`, 'post', {})
    }
    
    @ $mol_fiber.method
    meters() {
      return this.repo().domain().meter().list().filter( meter => meter.object().id() === this.id()  )
    }
    
  }

    _id?: string,

    ftp_sync_progress?: number,
    ftp_sync_updating?: boolean,
    ftp_sync_error?: string,
  }
